<Date>1490253440598</Date>< review>
Stopped in on Sunday on our way home from Indian Springs. I was excited because the reviews looked great and when we parked, it didn't appear to be too busy.

We waited at the hostess stand for at least three minutes before we were acknowledged. 75% of the tables were empty when we walked in but it didn't seem like anyone was working in the place besides one frazzled server. After he sat us, it took another five minutes to get water, another five after that to put in an order. Also, it was very unclear who was serving us.

We ordered the pesce fritto as an appetizer, which came out right away. my friend ordered a soup as an appetizer as well, but we had to ask for it. Our entrees were served about 20 minutes later.  I ordered a burger medium rare and it came out medium well. at that point, i just wanted to eat and go to bed, so i didn't feel like sending it back. who knows how much longer we would have sat there?

Anyway, the french fries are delicious and if you like to drink, it seems like a chill spot. Other than that, definitely two stars.<//review>

< review>
I took my wife there after she experienced a pretty severe allergic reaction to a prescribed antibiotic.
When we arrived I could smell a musty , moldy smell coming from the building. When we walked through the door the smell almost knocked us over. When we entered the waiting room we noticed that the overhead light fixtures were pretty much filthy. I was not allowed to accompany my wife for the consultation and examination because of "legal requirements". This has never happened to me before at any medical facility.
My wife said that when she walked down the hall to the examination room she passed two large fans blowing full blast. It was a hot day and apparently they have no air conditioning. She said both fans were filthy.

To be blunt, I felt guilty taking my wife there. Commonly practiced procedures for cleanliness are not in place there. The staff seemed to be just putting in their time. One was busy with her phone, either texting, FB, or gaming.

I will say that they got my wife in very quickly. In retrospect it was probably because most people know better than to go there, so the place was empty. When we left I had a horrible headache, probably from beathing whatever crap is growing in that building.

If you aren't sick when you get, there you will be by the time you leave.< /review>

<rating>5< /rating>< Review>
Excellent Experience.

We were looking everywhere in San Diego for persimmon trees, especially at the Home Depots and Lowes, but could not find any. However, I ended up googling Garden Nursery and Terra Bella Nursery showed up.

I called them to ask if there were any persimmon trees and the lady very nicely told me she would call back once she checks. She gives me a call back saying that there was and we ended up heading there.

Please note that we did not know what a Garden Nursery was. When we got there my parents and I were so surprised on how beautiful the Nursery was. This place was 10x better than your Lowes and Home Depot. I'm surprised that places like these existed and thank God for google to let us know of a place like this.

Anyways, huge selections of beautiful fruit trees and plants, but the main reason I'm writing this review is that the workers there are super helpful people honestly. Lady on the phone was so nice enough to check even though when I got there it was super busy. Cashier was nice and funny. And there was a guy who helped us put 2 persimmon trees inside our Van.

We're definitely coming back.<//Review>

Stopped by for breakfast with the family. Wasn't very crowded when we arrived at 8:30am but it started to get filled up about 30-45 minutes later.

< Review>
Love, love, LOVE this beach! Friendly dogs off leash playing and enjoying our amazing coast.
Sadly, there are some that come to visit and don't understand the concept of an off leash dog beach. Yes, the dogs will walk over your towel. Yes, they will eat your food if you put it on the towel on the ground. It is what it is. If this is going to bother you, there is a lovely beach less than a mile away called Avila, where you have no dog issues to worry about!<//Review>
